HSOLpt1prm_pxPrm_px = HSOLpt2prm_pxPrm_px*invxi2
HSOLprm_pxPrm_px = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_px + HSOLpt1Prm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_px + HSOLpt1prm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_px + HSOLpt1prm_pxPrm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_px = deltaT*(Qprm_pxPrm_px + sqrtQprm_pxPrm_px)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_px = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_px/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_px*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_px/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_px = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_px*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_px*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1prm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt1aPrm_px*sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt1aprm_px*sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2cprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt2dPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt2dprm_px*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2bprm_pxPrm_px = B*sxiprm_pxPrm_px
HSONLpt2aprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt2cprm_pxPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt1Prm_px*HSONLpt2bprm_px + HSONLpt1prm_px*HSONLpt2bPrm_px + HSONLpt1prm_pxPrm_px*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt2aPrm_px*svprm_px + HSONLpt2aprm_px*svPrm_px + HSONLpt2aprm_pxPrm_px*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_px = pxir*svprm_pxPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*svprm_px + pxirprm_px*svPrm_px
HSONLpt3bprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt3cPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_px*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt3bprm_pxPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pxPrm_px = B*HSONLpt2prm_pxPrm_px - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pxPrm_px
HSONLpt4eprm_pxPrm_px = snprm_pxPrm_px*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt4ePrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt4eprm_px*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt4eprm_pxPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt4dPrm_px*pxirprm_px + HSONLpt4dprm_px*pxirPrm_px + HSONLpt4dprm_pxPrm_px*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt4cprm_pxPrm_px*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLpt4bprm_pxPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pxPrm_px = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLpt3prm_pxPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pxPrm_px = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pxPrm_px + HSONLmultPrm_px*HSONLpt4prm_px + HSONLmultprm_px*HSONLpt4Prm_px + HSONLmultprm_pxPrm_px*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pxPrm_px = HSOLprm_pxPrm_px + HSONLprm_pxPrm_px + Hwcosprm_pxPrm_px*wcos + Hwrprm_pxPrm_px*wr + s3prm_pxPrm_px*w
Hsspt1prm_pxPrm_px = 3*sn*snprm_pxPrm_px + 3*snPrm_px*snprm_px - sx*sxprm_pxPrm_px - sxPrm_px*sxprm_px - sy*syprm_pxPrm_px - syPrm_px*syprm_px - sz*szprm_pxPrm_px - szPrm_px*szprm_px
Hssprm_pxPrm_px = Hsspt1prm_pxPrm_px*u3
Hprm_pxPrm_px = Hnsprm_pxPrm_px + Hsprm_pxPrm_px + Hssprm_pxPrm_px
Hrealprm_pxPrm_px = -HPrm_px*Hprm_px*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_px*Hprm_px*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pxPrm_px*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
pvrsqprm_pyPrm_px = 2*pvrPrm_px*pvrprm_py
pnsqprm_pyPrm_px = 2*pnPrm_px*pnprm_py
prsqprm_pyPrm_px = 2*prPrm_px*prprm_py
pxirsqprm_pyPrm_px = 2*pxirPrm_px*pxirprm_py
ptheta2prm_pyPrm_px = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pyPrm_px
prT4prm_pyPrm_px = 12*prT**2*prTPrm_px*prTprm_py
Hnspt4prm_pyPrm_px = Hnspt5*prT4prm_pyPrm_px + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_px*pfprm_py + Hnspt7*prsqprm_pyPrm_px + invrho2*ptheta2prm_pyPrm_px
Hnspt3prm_pyPrm_px = Hnspt4prm_pyPrm_px*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_pyPrm_px = Hnspt3prm_pyPrm_px*rho2
Hnsprm_pyPrm_px = Hnspt2prm_pyPrm_px*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2) - Hnspt2Prm_px*Hnspt2prm_py*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(4*Hnspt2**2)
Qprm_pyPrm_px = Qpt1*pvrsqprm_pyPrm_px + Qpt2*pxirsqprm_pyPrm_px + Qpt3*pnsqprm_pyPrm_px
pn2prm_pyPrm_px = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_pyPrm_px
ppprm_pyPrm_px = Qprm_pyPrm_px
sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_px = r*(-36*pn2prm_pyPrm_px + 3*ppprm_pyPrm_px)
sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_px = r*(-30*pn2prm_pyPrm_px + 4*ppprm_pyPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pyPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_px + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pyPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_px + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pyPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_px + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_px)
pn2ppprm_pyPrm_px = pn2*ppprm_pyPrm_px + pn2Prm_px*ppprm_py + pn2prm_py*ppPrm_px + pn2prm_pyPrm_px*pp
pp2prm_pyPrm_px = 2*pp*ppprm_pyPrm_px + 2*ppPrm_px*ppprm_py
pn2u2prm_pyPrm_px = pn2prm_pyPrm_px*u2
ppu2prm_pyPrm_px = ppprm_pyPrm_px*u2
pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_px = pn2ppprm_pyPrm_px*u2
sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_px = -720*pn2*pn2prm_pyPrm_px - 720*pn2Prm_px*pn2prm_py + 126*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_px + 3*pp2prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt5prm_pyPrm_px = -96*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_px + 23*pp2prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt4prm_pyPrm_px = 324*pn2prm_pyPrm_px - 120*ppprm_pyPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt3prm_pyPrm_px = -282*pn2prm_pyPrm_px + 206*ppprm_pyPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt5prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt2prm_pyPrm_px = r*sMultiplier1pt4prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt1prm_pyPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_pyPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_px = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1prm_pyPrm_px*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6prm_pyPrm_px = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_px/8 + 45*pn2Prm_px*pn2u2prm_py/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_px/8 + 45*pn2prm_py*pn2u2Prm_px/8 + 45*pn2prm_pyPrm_px*pn2u2/8
sMultiplier2pt5prm_pyPrm_px = pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_px/4 - 5*pp2prm_pyPrm_px*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4prm_pyPrm_px = -49*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_px/8 + 17*ppu2prm_pyPrm_px/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt3prm_pyPrm_px = -2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_px/3 - 109*ppu2prm_pyPrm_px/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt2prm_pyPrm_px = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt1prm_pyPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_pyPrm_px + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_pyPrm_px
sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier2pt1prm_pyPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pyPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pyPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pyPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_px*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pyPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_px
sxprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_px
syprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_px
szprm_pyPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_px
sxiprm_pyPrm_px = sxprm_pyPrm_px*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pyPrm_px*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pyPrm_px*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pyPrm_px = sxprm_pyPrm_px*vx + syprm_pyPrm_px*vy + szprm_pyPrm_px*vz
snprm_pyPrm_px = nx*sxprm_pyPrm_px + ny*syprm_pyPrm_px + nz*szprm_pyPrm_px
s3prm_pyPrm_px = e3USCOREx*sxprm_pyPrm_px + e3USCOREy*syprm_pyPrm_px + e3USCOREz*szprm_pyPrm_px
sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = Qprm_pyPrm_px/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_px*Qprm_py/(4*Q**(3/2))
oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = 2*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px
oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px - sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_px*sqrtQprm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_py*sqrtQPrm_px + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2 + 2*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_px*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_py/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**3
expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px = expMUsq*(Qprm_pyPrm_px + sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px)
Hwrpt4aprm_pyPrm_px = pxirsq*svprm_pyPrm_px + pxirsqPrm_px*svprm_py + pxirsqprm_py*svPrm_px + pxirsqprm_pyPrm_px*sv
Hwrpt4prm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt4aprm_pyPrm_px*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_pyPrm_px = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_px
Hwrpt3bprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt3cPrm_px*pvrprm_py + Hwrpt3cprm_py*pvrPrm_px + Hwrpt3cprm_pyPrm_px*pvr
Hwrpt3aprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt3bprm_pyPrm_px*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_pyPrm_px = B*Hwrpt3aprm_pyPrm_px
Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_px = deltaR*svprm_pyPrm_px
Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_px = snprm_pyPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt2fPrm_px*pvrprm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_py*pvrPrm_px + Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_px*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pyPrm_px + Hwrpt2gPrm_px*pnsqprm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_py*pnsqPrm_px + Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_px*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt2ePrm_px*pnprm_py + Hwrpt2eprm_py*pnPrm_px + Hwrpt2eprm_pyPrm_px*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_pyPrm_px = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_pyPrm_px + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_px*svprm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_py*svPrm_px + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_px = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pyPrm_px + Hwrpt2cprm_pyPrm_px - Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_px)
Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_px*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_px = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_px*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pyPrm_px = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_px - Hwrpt3prm_pyPrm_px + Hwrpt4prm_pyPrm_px) + Hwrpt1Prm_px*(Hwrpt2prm_py - Hwrpt3prm_py + Hwrpt4prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_py*(Hwrpt2Prm_px - Hwrpt3Prm_px + Hwrpt4Prm_px) + Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_px*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_px = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_px
Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_px = pvr*svprm_pyPrm_px + pvrPrm_px*svprm_py + pvrprm_py*svPrm_px
Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_px = B*Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_px - Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_px*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_px = Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_px = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px*xi2 + pvrsqprm_pyPrm_px
Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_px = Hwcospt6Prm_px*pnprm_py + Hwcospt6prm_py*pnPrm_px + Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_px*pn
Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_px = Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_px*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pyPrm_px
Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_px = -B*Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_px + Hwcospt3*snprm_pyPrm_px + Hwcospt3Prm_px*snprm_py + Hwcospt3prm_py*snPrm_px + Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_px*sn
Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_px = Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_px*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_pyPrm_px = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + Hwcospt1Prm_px*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_py + Hwcospt1prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_px + Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_px*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_px*deltaTsqrtQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_px = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pyPrm_px + HSOLpt3Prm_px*s3prm_py + HSOLpt3prm_py*s3Prm_px
HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_px = HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_px*invxi2
HSOLprm_pyPrm_px = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + HSOLpt1Prm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_py + HSOLpt1prm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_px + HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px = deltaT*(Qprm_pyPrm_px + sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_px*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_px = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_px*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_px*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1prm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt1aPrm_px*sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt1aprm_py*sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt2dPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt2dprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_px = B*sxiprm_pyPrm_px
HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt1Prm_px*HSONLpt2bprm_py + HSONLpt1prm_py*HSONLpt2bPrm_px + HSONLpt1prm_pyPrm_px*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt2aPrm_px*svprm_py + HSONLpt2aprm_py*svPrm_px + HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_px*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pyPrm_px = pxir*svprm_pyPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*svprm_py + pxirprm_py*svPrm_px
HSONLpt3bprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt3cPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_py*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_pyPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt3bprm_pyPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pyPrm_px = B*HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_px - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_px
HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_px = snprm_pyPrm_px*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt4ePrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt4eprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt4dPrm_px*pxirprm_py + HSONLpt4dprm_py*pxirPrm_px + HSONLpt4dprm_pyPrm_px*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt4cprm_pyPrm_px*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pyPrm_px = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLpt3prm_pyPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pyPrm_px = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pyPrm_px + HSONLmultPrm_px*HSONLpt4prm_py + HSONLmultprm_py*HSONLpt4Prm_px + HSONLmultprm_pyPrm_px*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pyPrm_px = HSOLprm_pyPrm_px + HSONLprm_pyPrm_px + Hwcosprm_pyPrm_px*wcos + Hwrprm_pyPrm_px*wr + s3prm_pyPrm_px*w
Hsspt1prm_pyPrm_px = 3*sn*snprm_pyPrm_px + 3*snPrm_px*snprm_py - sx*sxprm_pyPrm_px - sxPrm_px*sxprm_py - sy*syprm_pyPrm_px - syPrm_px*syprm_py - sz*szprm_pyPrm_px - szPrm_px*szprm_py
Hssprm_pyPrm_px = Hsspt1prm_pyPrm_px*u3
Hprm_pyPrm_px = Hnsprm_pyPrm_px + Hsprm_pyPrm_px + Hssprm_pyPrm_px
Hrealprm_pyPrm_px = -HPrm_px*Hprm_py*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_px*Hprm_py*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pyPrm_px*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
pvrsqprm_pzPrm_px = 2*pvrPrm_px*pvrprm_pz
pnsqprm_pzPrm_px = 2*pnPrm_px*pnprm_pz
prsqprm_pzPrm_px = 2*prPrm_px*prprm_pz
pxirsqprm_pzPrm_px = 2*pxirPrm_px*pxirprm_pz
ptheta2prm_pzPrm_px = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pzPrm_px
prT4prm_pzPrm_px = 12*prT**2*prTPrm_px*prTprm_pz
Hnspt4prm_pzPrm_px = Hnspt5*prT4prm_pzPrm_px + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_px*pfprm_pz + Hnspt7*prsqprm_pzPrm_px + invrho2*ptheta2prm_pzPrm_px
Hnspt3prm_pzPrm_px = Hnspt4prm_pzPrm_px*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_pzPrm_px = Hnspt3prm_pzPrm_px*rho2
Hnsprm_pzPrm_px = Hnspt2prm_pzPrm_px*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2) - Hnspt2Prm_px*Hnspt2prm_pz*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(4*Hnspt2**2)
Qprm_pzPrm_px = Qpt1*pvrsqprm_pzPrm_px + Qpt2*pxirsqprm_pzPrm_px + Qpt3*pnsqprm_pzPrm_px
pn2prm_pzPrm_px = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_pzPrm_px
ppprm_pzPrm_px = Qprm_pzPrm_px
sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_px = r*(-36*pn2prm_pzPrm_px + 3*ppprm_pzPrm_px)
sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_px = r*(-30*pn2prm_pzPrm_px + 4*ppprm_pzPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pzPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_px + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pzPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_px + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_px)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pzPrm_px = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_px + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_px)
pn2ppprm_pzPrm_px = pn2*ppprm_pzPrm_px + pn2Prm_px*ppprm_pz + pn2prm_pz*ppPrm_px + pn2prm_pzPrm_px*pp
pp2prm_pzPrm_px = 2*pp*ppprm_pzPrm_px + 2*ppPrm_px*ppprm_pz
pn2u2prm_pzPrm_px = pn2prm_pzPrm_px*u2
ppu2prm_pzPrm_px = ppprm_pzPrm_px*u2
pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_px = pn2ppprm_pzPrm_px*u2
sMultiplier1pt6prm_pzPrm_px = -720*pn2*pn2prm_pzPrm_px - 720*pn2Prm_px*pn2prm_pz + 126*pn2ppprm_pzPrm_px + 3*pp2prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt5prm_pzPrm_px = -96*pn2ppprm_pzPrm_px + 23*pp2prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt4prm_pzPrm_px = 324*pn2prm_pzPrm_px - 120*ppprm_pzPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt3prm_pzPrm_px = -282*pn2prm_pzPrm_px + 206*ppprm_pzPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt5prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt2prm_pzPrm_px = r*sMultiplier1pt4prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1pt1prm_pzPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_pzPrm_px + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_px = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1prm_pzPrm_px*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6prm_pzPrm_px = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_pzPrm_px/8 + 45*pn2Prm_px*pn2u2prm_pz/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_px/8 + 45*pn2prm_pz*pn2u2Prm_px/8 + 45*pn2prm_pzPrm_px*pn2u2/8
sMultiplier2pt5prm_pzPrm_px = pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_px/4 - 5*pp2prm_pzPrm_px*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4prm_pzPrm_px = -49*pn2u2prm_pzPrm_px/8 + 17*ppu2prm_pzPrm_px/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt3prm_pzPrm_px = -2*pn2u2prm_pzPrm_px/3 - 109*ppu2prm_pzPrm_px/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt2prm_pzPrm_px = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier2pt1prm_pzPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_pzPrm_px + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_pzPrm_px
sMultiplier2prm_pzPrm_px = eta*sMultiplier2pt1prm_pzPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pzPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pzPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pzPrm_px + sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_pzPrm_px*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pzPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pzPrm_px
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pzPrm_px
sxprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pzPrm_px
syprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pzPrm_px
szprm_pzPrm_px = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pzPrm_px
sxiprm_pzPrm_px = sxprm_pzPrm_px*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pzPrm_px*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pzPrm_px*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pzPrm_px = sxprm_pzPrm_px*vx + syprm_pzPrm_px*vy + szprm_pzPrm_px*vz
snprm_pzPrm_px = nx*sxprm_pzPrm_px + ny*syprm_pzPrm_px + nz*szprm_pzPrm_px
s3prm_pzPrm_px = e3USCOREx*sxprm_pzPrm_px + e3USCOREy*syprm_pzPrm_px + e3USCOREz*szprm_pzPrm_px
sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = Qprm_pzPrm_px/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_px*Qprm_pz/(4*Q**(3/2))
oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = 2*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px
oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px - sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_px*sqrtQprm_pz + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pz*sqrtQPrm_px + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2 + 2*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_px*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pz/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**3
expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px = expMUsq*(Qprm_pzPrm_px + sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px)
Hwrpt4aprm_pzPrm_px = pxirsq*svprm_pzPrm_px + pxirsqPrm_px*svprm_pz + pxirsqprm_pz*svPrm_px + pxirsqprm_pzPrm_px*sv
Hwrpt4prm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt4aprm_pzPrm_px*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_pzPrm_px = pxir*sxiprm_pzPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*sxiprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*sxiPrm_px
Hwrpt3bprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt3cPrm_px*pvrprm_pz + Hwrpt3cprm_pz*pvrPrm_px + Hwrpt3cprm_pzPrm_px*pvr
Hwrpt3aprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt3bprm_pzPrm_px*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_pzPrm_px = B*Hwrpt3aprm_pzPrm_px
Hwrpt2gprm_pzPrm_px = deltaR*svprm_pzPrm_px
Hwrpt2fprm_pzPrm_px = snprm_pzPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt2fPrm_px*pvrprm_pz + Hwrpt2fprm_pz*pvrPrm_px + Hwrpt2fprm_pzPrm_px*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pzPrm_px + Hwrpt2gPrm_px*pnsqprm_pz + Hwrpt2gprm_pz*pnsqPrm_px + Hwrpt2gprm_pzPrm_px*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt2ePrm_px*pnprm_pz + Hwrpt2eprm_pz*pnPrm_px + Hwrpt2eprm_pzPrm_px*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_pzPrm_px = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_pzPrm_px + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_px*svprm_pz + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pz*svPrm_px + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_pzPrm_px = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pzPrm_px + Hwrpt2cprm_pzPrm_px - Hwrpt2dprm_pzPrm_px)
Hwrpt2prm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt2aprm_pzPrm_px*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pzPrm_px = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt1bprm_pzPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt1aprm_pzPrm_px*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pzPrm_px = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pzPrm_px - Hwrpt3prm_pzPrm_px + Hwrpt4prm_pzPrm_px) + Hwrpt1Prm_px*(Hwrpt2prm_pz - Hwrpt3prm_pz + Hwrpt4prm_pz) + Hwrpt1prm_pz*(Hwrpt2Prm_px - Hwrpt3Prm_px + Hwrpt4Prm_px) + Hwrpt1prm_pzPrm_px*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pzPrm_px = pxir*sxiprm_pzPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*sxiprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*sxiPrm_px
Hwcospt8prm_pzPrm_px = pvr*svprm_pzPrm_px + pvrPrm_px*svprm_pz + pvrprm_pz*svPrm_px
Hwcospt7prm_pzPrm_px = B*Hwcospt8prm_pzPrm_px - Hwcospt9prm_pzPrm_px*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6prm_pzPrm_px = Hwcospt7prm_pzPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5prm_pzPrm_px = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px*xi2 + pvrsqprm_pzPrm_px
Hwcospt4prm_pzPrm_px = Hwcospt6Prm_px*pnprm_pz + Hwcospt6prm_pz*pnPrm_px + Hwcospt6prm_pzPrm_px*pn
Hwcospt3prm_pzPrm_px = Hwcospt5prm_pzPrm_px*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pzPrm_px
Hwcospt2prm_pzPrm_px = -B*Hwcospt4prm_pzPrm_px + Hwcospt3*snprm_pzPrm_px + Hwcospt3Prm_px*snprm_pz + Hwcospt3prm_pz*snPrm_px + Hwcospt3prm_pzPrm_px*sn
Hwcospt1prm_pzPrm_px = Hwcospt2prm_pzPrm_px*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_pzPrm_px = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + Hwcospt1Prm_px*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pz + Hwcospt1prm_pz*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_px + Hwcospt1prm_pzPrm_px*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_px*deltaTsqrtQprm_pz/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pzPrm_px = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pzPrm_px + HSOLpt3Prm_px*s3prm_pz + HSOLpt3prm_pz*s3Prm_px
HSOLpt1prm_pzPrm_px = HSOLpt2prm_pzPrm_px*invxi2
HSOLprm_pzPrm_px = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + HSOLpt1Prm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pz + HSOLpt1prm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_px + HSOLpt1prm_pzPrm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px = deltaT*(Qprm_pzPrm_px + sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_px*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pz/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pzPrm_px = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_px*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLmult2prm_pzPrm_px*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1prm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt1aPrm_px*sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt1aprm_pz*sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2cprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt2dPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt2dprm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px
HSONLpt2bprm_pzPrm_px = B*sxiprm_pzPrm_px
HSONLpt2aprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt2cprm_pzPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt1Prm_px*HSONLpt2bprm_pz + HSONLpt1prm_pz*HSONLpt2bPrm_px + HSONLpt1prm_pzPrm_px*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt2aPrm_px*svprm_pz + HSONLpt2aprm_pz*svPrm_px + HSONLpt2aprm_pzPrm_px*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pzPrm_px = pxir*svprm_pzPrm_px + pxirPrm_px*svprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*svPrm_px
HSONLpt3bprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt3cPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt3cprm_pz*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_pzPrm_px*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt3bprm_pzPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pzPrm_px = B*HSONLpt2prm_pzPrm_px - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pzPrm_px
HSONLpt4eprm_pzPrm_px = snprm_pzPrm_px*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt4ePrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt4eprm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_px + HSONLpt4eprm_pzPrm_px*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt4dPrm_px*pxirprm_pz + HSONLpt4dprm_pz*pxirPrm_px + HSONLpt4dprm_pzPrm_px*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt4cprm_pzPrm_px*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLpt4bprm_pzPrm_px*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pzPrm_px = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLpt3prm_pzPrm_px*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pzPrm_px = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pzPrm_px + HSONLmultPrm_px*HSONLpt4prm_pz + HSONLmultprm_pz*HSONLpt4Prm_px + HSONLmultprm_pzPrm_px*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pzPrm_px = HSOLprm_pzPrm_px + HSONLprm_pzPrm_px + Hwcosprm_pzPrm_px*wcos + Hwrprm_pzPrm_px*wr + s3prm_pzPrm_px*w
Hsspt1prm_pzPrm_px = 3*sn*snprm_pzPrm_px + 3*snPrm_px*snprm_pz - sx*sxprm_pzPrm_px - sxPrm_px*sxprm_pz - sy*syprm_pzPrm_px - syPrm_px*syprm_pz - sz*szprm_pzPrm_px - szPrm_px*szprm_pz
Hssprm_pzPrm_px = Hsspt1prm_pzPrm_px*u3
Hprm_pzPrm_px = Hnsprm_pzPrm_px + Hsprm_pzPrm_px + Hssprm_pzPrm_px
Hrealprm_pzPrm_px = -HPrm_px*Hprm_pz*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_px*Hprm_pz*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pzPrm_px*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
prTPrm_py = csi2*ny
prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py = prTPrm_py*(1 - 1/csi1)
tmppxPrm_py = -nx*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py
tmppyPrm_py = -ny*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py + 1
tmppzPrm_py = -nz*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py
pxirPrm_py = r*(tmppxPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_py*xiUSCOREz)
pvrPrm_py = r*(tmppxPrm_py*vx + tmppyPrm_py*vy + tmppzPrm_py*vz)
pvrsqPrm_py = 2*pvr*pvrPrm_py
pnPrm_py = nx*tmppxPrm_py + ny*tmppyPrm_py + nz*tmppzPrm_py
pnsqPrm_py = 2*pn*pnPrm_py
prPrm_py = pnPrm_py
prsqPrm_py = 2*pr*prPrm_py
pfPrm_py = pxirPrm_py
pxirsqPrm_py = 2*pxir*pxirPrm_py
ptheta2Prm_py = invxi2*pvrsqPrm_py
prT4Prm_py = 4*prT**3*prTPrm_py
Hnspt4Prm_py = Hnspt5*prT4Prm_py + 2*Hnspt6*pf*pfPrm_py + Hnspt7*prsqPrm_py + invrho2*ptheta2Prm_py
Hnspt3Prm_py = Hnspt4Prm_py*deltaT
Hnspt2Prm_py = Hnspt3Prm_py*rho2
Hnspt1Prm_py = pfPrm_py*ww
HnsPrm_py = Hnspt1Prm_py*invLamb + Hnspt2Prm_py*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2)
QPrm_py = Qpt1*pvrsqPrm_py + Qpt2*pxirsqPrm_py + Qpt3*pnsqPrm_py
pn2Prm_py = deltaR*invrho2*prsqPrm_py
ppPrm_py = QPrm_py
sKerrmultfactPrm_py = r*(-36*pn2Prm_py + 3*ppPrm_py)
sStarmultfactPrm_py = r*(-30*pn2Prm_py + 4*ppPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1Prm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1Prm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1Prm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
pn2ppPrm_py = pn2*ppPrm_py + pn2Prm_py*pp
pp2Prm_py = 2*pp*ppPrm_py
pn2u2Prm_py = pn2Prm_py*u2
ppu2Prm_py = ppPrm_py*u2
pn2ppu2Prm_py = pn2ppPrm_py*u2
sMultiplier1pt6Prm_py = -720*pn2*pn2Prm_py + 126*pn2ppPrm_py + 3*pp2Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt5Prm_py = -96*pn2ppPrm_py + 23*pp2Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt4Prm_py = 324*pn2Prm_py - 120*ppPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt6Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt3Prm_py = -282*pn2Prm_py + 206*ppPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt5Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt2Prm_py = r*sMultiplier1pt4Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt1Prm_py = eta*sMultiplier1pt2Prm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt3Prm_py
sMultiplier1Prm_py = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1Prm_py*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6Prm_py = 45*pn2*pn2u2Prm_py/8 + 45*pn2Prm_py*pn2u2/8 - 13*pn2ppu2Prm_py/8
sMultiplier2pt5Prm_py = pn2ppu2Prm_py/4 - 5*pp2Prm_py*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4Prm_py = -49*pn2u2Prm_py/8 + 17*ppu2Prm_py/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt3Prm_py = -2*pn2u2Prm_py/3 - 109*ppu2Prm_py/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt2Prm_py = r*sMultiplier2pt4Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt1Prm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt2Prm_py + r*sMultiplier2pt3Prm_py
sMultiplier2Prm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt1Prm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2Prm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1Prm_py + sMultiplier1Prm_py*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2Prm_py*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2Prm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1Prm_py + sMultiplier1Prm_py*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2Prm_py*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2Prm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1Prm_py + sMultiplier1Prm_py*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2Prm_py*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2Prm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2Prm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2Prm_py
sxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExPrm_py
syPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyPrm_py
szPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzPrm_py
sxiPrm_py = sxPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + syPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + szPrm_py*xiUSCOREz
svPrm_py = sxPrm_py*vx + syPrm_py*vy + szPrm_py*vz
snPrm_py = nx*sxPrm_py + ny*syPrm_py + nz*szPrm_py
s3Prm_py = e3USCOREx*sxPrm_py + e3USCOREy*syPrm_py + e3USCOREz*szPrm_py
sqrtQPrm_py = QPrm_py/(2*sp.sqrt(Q))
oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py = 2*sqrtQPrm_py
oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py = oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py - sqrtQPrm_py
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2
expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py = expMUsq*(QPrm_py + sqrtQPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aPrm_py = pxirsq*svPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4Prm_py = Hwrpt4aPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cPrm_py = pxir*sxiPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxi
Hwrpt3bPrm_py = Hwrpt3c*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt3cPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt3aPrm_py = Hwrpt3bPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3Prm_py = B*Hwrpt3aPrm_py
Hwrpt2gPrm_py = deltaR*svPrm_py
Hwrpt2fPrm_py = snPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2ePrm_py = Hwrpt2f*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt2fPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt2dPrm_py = Hwrpt2g*pnsqPrm_py + Hwrpt2gPrm_py*pnsq
Hwrpt2cPrm_py = Hwrpt2e*pnPrm_py + Hwrpt2ePrm_py*pn
Hwrpt2bPrm_py = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt2aPrm_py = xi2*(Hwrpt2bPrm_py + Hwrpt2cPrm_py - Hwrpt2dPrm_py)
Hwrpt2Prm_py = Hwrpt2aPrm_py*deltaT
Hwrpt1bPrm_py = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py*invxi2
Hwrpt1aPrm_py = Hwrpt1bPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1Prm_py = Hwrpt1aPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
HwrPrm_py = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2Prm_py - Hwrpt3Prm_py + Hwrpt4Prm_py) + Hwrpt1Prm_py*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9Prm_py = pxir*sxiPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxi
Hwcospt8Prm_py = pvr*svPrm_py + pvrPrm_py*sv
Hwcospt7Prm_py = B*Hwcospt8Prm_py - Hwcospt9Prm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6Prm_py = Hwcospt7Prm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5Prm_py = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py*xi2 + pvrsqPrm_py
Hwcospt4Prm_py = Hwcospt6*pnPrm_py + Hwcospt6Prm_py*pn
Hwcospt3Prm_py = Hwcospt5Prm_py*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqPrm_py
Hwcospt2Prm_py = -B*Hwcospt4Prm_py + Hwcospt3*snPrm_py + Hwcospt3Prm_py*sn
Hwcospt1Prm_py = Hwcospt2Prm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
HwcosPrm_py = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py + Hwcospt1Prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQPrm_py = deltaT*sqrtQPrm_py
invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**2
HSOLpt5Prm_py = pxirPrm_py*(-B + expMUexpnu)
HSOLpt4Prm_py = HSOLpt5Prm_py*invexpMU
HSOLpt3Prm_py = HSOLpt4Prm_py*expnusq
HSOLpt2Prm_py = HSOLpt3*s3Prm_py + HSOLpt3Prm_py*s3
HSOLpt1Prm_py = HSOLpt2Prm_py*invxi2
HSOLPrm_py = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_py + HSOLpt1Prm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_py = deltaT*(QPrm_py + sqrtQPrm_py)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2
HSONLmult2Prm_py = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_py*invxi2
HSONLmultPrm_py = HSONLmult2Prm_py*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1bPrm_py = pnPrm_py*xi2
HSONLpt1aPrm_py = HSONLpt1bPrm_py*(-mucos + nucos) + mur*pvrPrm_py - nur*pvrPrm_py
HSONLpt1Prm_py = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt1aPrm_py*sqrtQ - HSONLpt1bPrm_py*mucos + mur*pvrPrm_py
HSONLpt2dPrm_py = nur*pxirPrm_py
HSONLpt2cPrm_py = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt2dPrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt2bPrm_py = B*sxiPrm_py
HSONLpt2aPrm_py = HSONLpt2cPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2Prm_py = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bPrm_py + HSONLpt1Prm_py*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svPrm_py + HSONLpt2aPrm_py*sv
HSONLpt3cPrm_py = pxir*svPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sv
HSONLpt3bPrm_py = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt3cPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aPrm_py = HSONLpt3bPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3Prm_py = B*HSONLpt2Prm_py - BR*HSONLpt3aPrm_py
HSONLpt4ePrm_py = snPrm_py*xi2
HSONLpt4dPrm_py = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt4ePrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cPrm_py = HSONLpt4d*pxirPrm_py + HSONLpt4dPrm_py*pxir
HSONLpt4bPrm_py = HSONLpt4cPrm_py*nucos
HSONLpt4aPrm_py = HSONLpt4bPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4Prm_py = -B*HSONLpt4aPrm_py + HSONLpt3Prm_py*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLPrm_py = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4Prm_py + HSONLmultPrm_py*HSONLpt4
HsPrm_py = HSOLPrm_py + HSONLPrm_py + HwcosPrm_py*wcos + HwrPrm_py*wr + s3Prm_py*w
Hsspt1Prm_py = 3*sn*snPrm_py - sx*sxPrm_py - sy*syPrm_py - sz*szPrm_py
HssPrm_py = Hsspt1Prm_py*u3
HPrm_py = HnsPrm_py + HsPrm_py + HssPrm_py
HrealPrm_py = HPrm_py*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
prTprm_xPrm_py = csi2*nyprm_x + csi2prm_x*ny
prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_py = prTprm_xPrm_py*(1 - 1/csi1) + csi1prm_x*prTPrm_py/csi1**2
tmppxprm_xPrm_py = -nx*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_py - nxprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py
tmppyprm_xPrm_py = -ny*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_py - nyprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py
tmppzprm_xPrm_py = -nz*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_py - nzprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_py
pxirprm_xPrm_py = r*(tmppxPrm_py*xiUSCORExprm_x + tmppxprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_py*xiUSCOREyprm_x + tmppyprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_py*xiUSCOREzprm_x + tmppzprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREz) + rprm_x*(tmppxPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_py*xiUSCOREz)
pvrprm_xPrm_py = r*(tmppxPrm_py*vxprm_x + tmppxprm_xPrm_py*vx + tmppyPrm_py*vyprm_x + tmppyprm_xPrm_py*vy + tmppzPrm_py*vzprm_x + tmppzprm_xPrm_py*vz) + rprm_x*(tmppxPrm_py*vx + tmppyPrm_py*vy + tmppzPrm_py*vz)
pvrsqprm_xPrm_py = 2*pvr*pvrprm_xPrm_py + 2*pvrPrm_py*pvrprm_x
pnprm_xPrm_py = nx*tmppxprm_xPrm_py + nxprm_x*tmppxPrm_py + ny*tmppyprm_xPrm_py + nyprm_x*tmppyPrm_py + nz*tmppzprm_xPrm_py + nzprm_x*tmppzPrm_py
pnsqprm_xPrm_py = 2*pn*pnprm_xPrm_py + 2*pnPrm_py*pnprm_x
prprm_xPrm_py = pnprm_xPrm_py
prsqprm_xPrm_py = 2*pr*prprm_xPrm_py + 2*prPrm_py*prprm_x
pfprm_xPrm_py = pxirprm_xPrm_py
pxirsqprm_xPrm_py = 2*pxir*pxirprm_xPrm_py + 2*pxirPrm_py*pxirprm_x
ptheta2prm_xPrm_py = invxi2*pvrsqprm_xPrm_py + invxi2prm_x*pvrsqPrm_py
prT4prm_xPrm_py = 4*prT**3*prTprm_xPrm_py + 12*prT**2*prTPrm_py*prTprm_x
Hnspt4prm_xPrm_py = Hnspt5*prT4prm_xPrm_py + Hnspt5prm_x*prT4Prm_py + 2*Hnspt6*pf*pfprm_xPrm_py + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_py*pfprm_x + 2*Hnspt6prm_x*pf*pfPrm_py + Hnspt7*prsqprm_xPrm_py + Hnspt7prm_x*prsqPrm_py + invrho2*ptheta2prm_xPrm_py + invrho2prm_x*ptheta2Prm_py
Hnspt3prm_xPrm_py = Hnspt4Prm_py*deltaTprm_x + Hnspt4prm_xPrm_py*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_xPrm_py = Hnspt3Prm_py*rho2prm_x + Hnspt3prm_xPrm_py*rho2
Hnspt1prm_xPrm_py = pfPrm_py*wwprm_x + pfprm_xPrm_py*ww
Hnsprm_xPrm_py = Hnspt1Prm_py*invLambprm_x + Hnspt1prm_xPrm_py*invLamb + sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)*(Hnspt2Prm_py*invLambprm_x/2 + Hnspt2prm_xPrm_py*invLamb/2)/(Hnspt2*invLamb) - Hnspt2Prm_py*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)*(Hnspt2*invLambprm_x/2 + Hnspt2prm_x*invLamb/2)/(2*Hnspt2**2*invLamb)
Qprm_xPrm_py = Qpt1*pvrsqprm_xPrm_py + Qpt1prm_x*pvrsqPrm_py + Qpt2*pxirsqprm_xPrm_py + Qpt2prm_x*pxirsqPrm_py + Qpt3*pnsqprm_xPrm_py + Qpt3prm_x*pnsqPrm_py
pn2prm_xPrm_py = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_xPrm_py + deltaR*invrho2prm_x*prsqPrm_py + deltaRprm_x*invrho2*prsqPrm_py
ppprm_xPrm_py = Qprm_xPrm_py
sKerrmultfactprm_xPrm_py = r*(-36*pn2prm_xPrm_py + 3*ppprm_xPrm_py) + rprm_x*(-36*pn2Prm_py + 3*ppPrm_py)
sStarmultfactprm_xPrm_py = r*(-30*pn2prm_xPrm_py + 4*ppprm_xPrm_py) + rprm_x*(-30*pn2Prm_py + 4*ppPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_xPrm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactprm_xPrm_py + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactprm_xPrm_py) + etaover12rprm_x*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_xPrm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactprm_xPrm_py + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactprm_xPrm_py) + etaover12rprm_x*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_xPrm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_xPrm_py + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_xPrm_py) + etaover12rprm_x*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactPrm_py + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactPrm_py)
pn2ppprm_xPrm_py = pn2*ppprm_xPrm_py + pn2Prm_py*ppprm_x + pn2prm_x*ppPrm_py + pn2prm_xPrm_py*pp
pp2prm_xPrm_py = 2*pp*ppprm_xPrm_py + 2*ppPrm_py*ppprm_x
pn2u2prm_xPrm_py = pn2Prm_py*u2prm_x + pn2prm_xPrm_py*u2
ppu2prm_xPrm_py = ppPrm_py*u2prm_x + ppprm_xPrm_py*u2
pn2ppu2prm_xPrm_py = pn2ppPrm_py*u2prm_x + pn2ppprm_xPrm_py*u2
sMultiplier1pt6prm_xPrm_py = -720*pn2*pn2prm_xPrm_py - 720*pn2Prm_py*pn2prm_x + 126*pn2ppprm_xPrm_py + 3*pp2prm_xPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt5prm_xPrm_py = -96*pn2ppprm_xPrm_py + 23*pp2prm_xPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt4prm_xPrm_py = 324*pn2prm_xPrm_py - 120*ppprm_xPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier1pt6Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt3prm_xPrm_py = -282*pn2prm_xPrm_py + 206*ppprm_xPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt5prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier1pt5Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt2prm_xPrm_py = r*sMultiplier1pt4prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier1pt4Prm_py
sMultiplier1pt1prm_xPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_xPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier1pt3Prm_py
sMultiplier1prm_xPrm_py = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1Prm_py*u2prm_x/72 - eta*sMultiplier1pt1prm_xPrm_py*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6prm_xPrm_py = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_xPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2Prm_py*pn2u2prm_x/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_xPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_x*pn2u2Prm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_xPrm_py*pn2u2/8
sMultiplier2pt5prm_xPrm_py = pn2ppu2prm_xPrm_py/4 - 5*pp2Prm_py*u2prm_x/16 - 5*pp2prm_xPrm_py*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4prm_xPrm_py = -49*pn2u2prm_xPrm_py/8 + 17*ppu2prm_xPrm_py/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier2pt6Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt3prm_xPrm_py = -2*pn2u2prm_xPrm_py/3 - 109*ppu2prm_xPrm_py/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier2pt5Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt2prm_xPrm_py = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier2pt4Prm_py
sMultiplier2pt1prm_xPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_xPrm_py + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_xPrm_py + rprm_x*sMultiplier2pt3Prm_py
sMultiplier2prm_xPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt1prm_xPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_xPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_xPrm_py*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_xPrm_py*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_xPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_xPrm_py*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2prm_xPrm_py*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_xPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_xPrm_py*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_xPrm_py*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_xPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_xPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_xPrm_py
sxprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_xPrm_py
syprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_xPrm_py
szprm_xPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_xPrm_py
sxiprm_xPrm_py = sxPrm_py*xiUSCORExprm_x + sxprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + syPrm_py*xiUSCOREyprm_x + syprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + szPrm_py*xiUSCOREzprm_x + szprm_xPrm_py*xiUSCOREz
svprm_xPrm_py = sxPrm_py*vxprm_x + sxprm_xPrm_py*vx + syPrm_py*vyprm_x + syprm_xPrm_py*vy + szPrm_py*vzprm_x + szprm_xPrm_py*vz
snprm_xPrm_py = nx*sxprm_xPrm_py + nxprm_x*sxPrm_py + ny*syprm_xPrm_py + nyprm_x*syPrm_py + nz*szprm_xPrm_py + nzprm_x*szPrm_py
s3prm_xPrm_py = e3USCOREx*sxprm_xPrm_py + e3USCOREy*syprm_xPrm_py + e3USCOREz*szprm_xPrm_py
sqrtQprm_xPrm_py = Qprm_xPrm_py/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_py*Qprm_x/(4*Q**(3/2))
oneplus2sqrtQprm_xPrm_py = 2*sqrtQprm_xPrm_py
oneplus1sqrtQprm_xPrm_py = oneplus2sqrtQprm_xPrm_py - sqrtQprm_xPrm_py
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_xPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_xPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQprm_x + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_x*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_xPrm_py*sqrtQ + 2*Bprm_x*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*Bprm_x*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_xPrm_py = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_xPrm_py/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2 + 2*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_x/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**3
expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_xPrm_py = expMUsq*(Qprm_xPrm_py + sqrtQprm_xPrm_py) + expMUsqprm_x*(QPrm_py + sqrtQPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aprm_xPrm_py = pxirsq*svprm_xPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*svprm_x + pxirsqprm_x*svPrm_py + pxirsqprm_xPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4prm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt4aPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusqprm_x + Hwrpt4aprm_xPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_xPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_xPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_x + pxirprm_x*sxiPrm_py + pxirprm_xPrm_py*sxi
Hwrpt3bprm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt3c*pvrprm_xPrm_py + Hwrpt3cPrm_py*pvrprm_x + Hwrpt3cprm_x*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt3cprm_xPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt3aprm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt3bPrm_py*expMUexpnuprm_x + Hwrpt3bprm_xPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_xPrm_py = B*Hwrpt3aprm_xPrm_py + Bprm_x*Hwrpt3aPrm_py
Hwrpt2gprm_xPrm_py = deltaR*svprm_xPrm_py + deltaRprm_x*svPrm_py
Hwrpt2fprm_xPrm_py = snPrm_py*sqrtdeltaRprm_x + snprm_xPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt2f*pvrprm_xPrm_py + Hwrpt2fPrm_py*pvrprm_x + Hwrpt2fprm_x*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_xPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_xPrm_py + Hwrpt2gPrm_py*pnsqprm_x + Hwrpt2gprm_x*pnsqPrm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_xPrm_py*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_xPrm_py = Hwrpt2e*pnprm_xPrm_py + Hwrpt2ePrm_py*pnprm_x + Hwrpt2eprm_x*pnPrm_py + Hwrpt2eprm_xPrm_py*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_xPrm_py = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_xPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py*svprm_x + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_x*svPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_xPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_xPrm_py = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_xPrm_py + Hwrpt2cprm_xPrm_py - Hwrpt2dprm_xPrm_py) + xi2prm_x*(Hwrpt2bPrm_py + Hwrpt2cPrm_py - Hwrpt2dPrm_py)

Hwcospt8prm_xPrm_py = pvr*svprm_xPrm_py + pvrPrm_py*svprm_x + pvrprm_x*svPrm_py + pvrprm_xPrm_py*sv
Hwcospt7prm_xPrm_py = B*Hwcospt8prm_xPrm_py + Bprm_x*Hwcospt8Prm_py - Hwcospt9Prm_py*expMUexpnuprm_x - Hwcospt9prm_xPrm_py*expMUexpnu

Hwcospt2prm_xPrm_py = -B*Hwcospt4prm_xPrm_py - Bprm_x*Hwcospt4Prm_py + Hwcospt3*snprm_xPrm_py + Hwcospt3Prm_py*snprm_x + Hwcospt3prm_x*snPrm_py + Hwcospt3prm_xPrm_py*sn
Hwcospt1prm_xPrm_py = Hwcospt2Prm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnuprm_x + Hwcospt2prm_xPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_xPrm_py = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_xPrm_py + Hwcospt1Prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_x + Hwcospt1prm_x*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py + Hwcospt1prm_xPrm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_xPrm_py = deltaT*sqrtQprm_xPrm_py + deltaTprm_x*sqrtQPrm_py
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_xPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQprm_xPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_py*deltaTsqrtQprm_x/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt5prm_xPrm_py = pxirPrm_py*(-Bprm_x + expMUexpnuprm_x) + pxirprm_xPrm_py*(-B + expMUexpnu)

HSONLpt3cprm_xPrm_py = pxir*svprm_xPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*svprm_x + pxirprm_x*svPrm_py + pxirprm_xPrm_py*sv
HSONLpt3bprm_xPrm_py = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_xPrm_py + HSONLpt3cPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQprm_x + HSONLpt3cprm_x*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_xPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQ

prTprm_yPrm_py = csi2*nyprm_y + csi2prm_y*ny

szprm_zPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_zPrm_py

s3prm_zPrm_py = e3USCOREx*sxprm_zPrm_py + e3USCOREy*syprm_zPrm_py + e3USCOREz*szprm_zPrm_py
sqrtQprm_zPrm_py = Qprm_zPrm_py/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_py*Qprm_z/(4*Q**(3/2))

twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_zPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_zPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQprm_z + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_z*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_zPrm_py*sqrtQ + 2*Bprm_z*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*Bprm_z*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQ

expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_zPrm_py = expMUsq*(Qprm_zPrm_py + sqrtQprm_zPrm_py) + expMUsqprm_z*(QPrm_py + sqrtQPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aprm_zPrm_py = pxirsq*svprm_zPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*svprm_z + pxirsqprm_z*svPrm_py + pxirsqprm_zPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4prm_zPrm_py = Hwrpt4aPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusqprm_z + Hwrpt4aprm_zPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq

Hrealprm_zPrm_py = -HPrm_py*Hprm_z*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_py*Hprm_z*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_zPrm_py*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)

sMultiplier2pt4prm_pxPrm_py = -49*pn2u2prm_pxPrm_py/8 + 17*ppu2prm_pxPrm_py/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6prm_pxPrm_py

sMultiplier2pt2prm_pxPrm_py = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pxPrm_py
sMultiplier2pt1prm_pxPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_pxPrm_py + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_pxPrm_py
sMultiplier2prm_pxPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt1prm_pxPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pxPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pxPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pxPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_pxPrm_py*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pxPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pxPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pxPrm_py
sxprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pxPrm_py
syprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pxPrm_py
szprm_pxPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pxPrm_py
sxiprm_pxPrm_py = sxprm_pxPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pxPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pxPrm_py*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pxPrm_py = sxprm_pxPrm_py*vx + syprm_pxPrm_py*vy + szprm_pxPrm_py*vz
snprm_pxPrm_py = nx*sxprm_pxPrm_py + ny*syprm_pxPrm_py + nz*szprm_pxPrm_py
s3prm_pxPrm_py = e3USCOREx*sxprm_pxPrm_py + e3USCOREy*syprm_pxPrm_py + e3USCOREz*szprm_pxPrm_py
sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = Qprm_pxPrm_py/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_py*Qprm_px/(4*Q**(3/2))
oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = 2*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py
oneplus1sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py - sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQprm_px + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_px*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2 + 2*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py*twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_px/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**3
expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_py = expMUsq*(Qprm_pxPrm_py + sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aprm_pxPrm_py = pxirsq*svprm_pxPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*svprm_px + pxirsqprm_px*svPrm_py + pxirsqprm_pxPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4prm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt4aprm_pxPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_pxPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pxPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_px + pxirprm_px*sxiPrm_py
Hwrpt3bprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt3cPrm_py*pvrprm_px + Hwrpt3cprm_px*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt3cprm_pxPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt3aprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt3bprm_pxPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_pxPrm_py = B*Hwrpt3aprm_pxPrm_py
Hwrpt2gprm_pxPrm_py = deltaR*svprm_pxPrm_py
Hwrpt2fprm_pxPrm_py = snprm_pxPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt2fPrm_py*pvrprm_px + Hwrpt2fprm_px*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_pxPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pxPrm_py + Hwrpt2gPrm_py*pnsqprm_px + Hwrpt2gprm_px*pnsqPrm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_pxPrm_py*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt2ePrm_py*pnprm_px + Hwrpt2eprm_px*pnPrm_py + Hwrpt2eprm_pxPrm_py*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_pxPrm_py = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_pxPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py*svprm_px + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_px*svPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_pxPrm_py = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pxPrm_py + Hwrpt2cprm_pxPrm_py - Hwrpt2dprm_pxPrm_py)
Hwrpt2prm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt2aprm_pxPrm_py*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pxPrm_py = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt1bprm_pxPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt1aprm_pxPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pxPrm_py = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pxPrm_py - Hwrpt3prm_pxPrm_py + Hwrpt4prm_pxPrm_py) + Hwrpt1Prm_py*(Hwrpt2prm_px - Hwrpt3prm_px + Hwrpt4prm_px) + Hwrpt1prm_px*(Hwrpt2Prm_py - Hwrpt3Prm_py + Hwrpt4Prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_pxPrm_py*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pxPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pxPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_px + pxirprm_px*sxiPrm_py
Hwcospt8prm_pxPrm_py = pvr*svprm_pxPrm_py + pvrPrm_py*svprm_px + pvrprm_px*svPrm_py
Hwcospt7prm_pxPrm_py = B*Hwcospt8prm_pxPrm_py - Hwcospt9prm_pxPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6prm_pxPrm_py = Hwcospt7prm_pxPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5prm_pxPrm_py = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_py*xi2 + pvrsqprm_pxPrm_py
Hwcospt4prm_pxPrm_py = Hwcospt6Prm_py*pnprm_px + Hwcospt6prm_px*pnPrm_py + Hwcospt6prm_pxPrm_py*pn
Hwcospt3prm_pxPrm_py = Hwcospt5prm_pxPrm_py*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pxPrm_py
Hwcospt2prm_pxPrm_py = -B*Hwcospt4prm_pxPrm_py + Hwcospt3*snprm_pxPrm_py + Hwcospt3Prm_py*snprm_px + Hwcospt3prm_px*snPrm_py + Hwcospt3prm_pxPrm_py*sn
Hwcospt1prm_pxPrm_py = Hwcospt2prm_pxPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_pxPrm_py = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py + Hwcospt1Prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_px + Hwcospt1prm_px*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py + Hwcospt1prm_pxPrm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_py*deltaTsqrtQprm_px/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pxPrm_py = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pxPrm_py + HSOLpt3Prm_py*s3prm_px + HSOLpt3prm_px*s3Prm_py

deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_py = deltaT*(Qprm_pxPrm_py + sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py)

HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_py = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_py*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pxPrm_py = HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_py*expnuinvexpMU2

HSONLpt2cprm_pxPrm_py = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py + HSONLpt2dPrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt2dprm_px*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py
HSONLpt2bprm_pxPrm_py = B*sxiprm_pxPrm_py

HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_py = pxir*svprm_pxPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*svprm_px + pxirprm_px*svPrm_py
HSONLpt3bprm_pxPrm_py = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pxPrm_py + HSONLpt3cPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_px*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQ

HSONLpt4bprm_pxPrm_py = HSONLpt4cprm_pxPrm_py*nucos

Hsprm_pxPrm_py = HSOLprm_pxPrm_py + HSONLprm_pxPrm_py + Hwcosprm_pxPrm_py*wcos + Hwrprm_pxPrm_py*wr + s3prm_pxPrm_py*w
Hsspt1prm_pxPrm_py = 3*sn*snprm_pxPrm_py + 3*snPrm_py*snprm_px - sx*sxprm_pxPrm_py - sxPrm_py*sxprm_px - sy*syprm_pxPrm_py - syPrm_py*syprm_px - sz*szprm_pxPrm_py - szPrm_py*szprm_px

Hrealprm_pxPrm_py = -HPrm_py*Hprm_px*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_py*Hprm_px*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pxPrm_py*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
pvrsqprm_pyPrm_py = 2*pvrPrm_py*pvrprm_py
pnsqprm_pyPrm_py = 2*pnPrm_py*pnprm_py
prsqprm_pyPrm_py = 2*prPrm_py*prprm_py
pxirsqprm_pyPrm_py = 2*pxirPrm_py*pxirprm_py
ptheta2prm_pyPrm_py = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pyPrm_py

Hnspt2prm_pyPrm_py = Hnspt3prm_pyPrm_py*rho2

ppprm_pyPrm_py = Qprm_pyPrm_py
sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_py = r*(-36*pn2prm_pyPrm_py + 3*ppprm_pyPrm_py)

sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_py = -720*pn2*pn2prm_pyPrm_py - 720*pn2Prm_py*pn2prm_py + 126*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_py + 3*pp2prm_pyPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt5prm_pyPrm_py = -96*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_py + 23*pp2prm_pyPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt4prm_pyPrm_py = 324*pn2prm_pyPrm_py - 120*ppprm_pyPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_py

sMultiplier1pt1prm_pyPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_pyPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_pyPrm_py

sMultiplier2pt6prm_pyPrm_py = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2Prm_py*pn2u2prm_py/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_py*pn2u2Prm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_pyPrm_py*pn2u2/8

sMultiplier2pt3prm_pyPrm_py = -2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_py/3 - 109*ppu2prm_pyPrm_py/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5prm_pyPrm_py
sMultiplier2pt2prm_pyPrm_py = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pyPrm_py

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pyPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_py*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_py*sigmaKerr0

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pyPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_py*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_py*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pyPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_py
sxprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_py
syprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_py
szprm_pyPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_py
sxiprm_pyPrm_py = sxprm_pyPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pyPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pyPrm_py*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pyPrm_py = sxprm_pyPrm_py*vx + syprm_pyPrm_py*vy + szprm_pyPrm_py*vz

oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py = 2*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py
oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py - sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQprm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_py*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py*sqrtQ

expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py = expMUsq*(Qprm_pyPrm_py + sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aprm_pyPrm_py = pxirsq*svprm_pyPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*svprm_py + pxirsqprm_py*svPrm_py + pxirsqprm_pyPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4prm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt4aprm_pyPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_pyPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_py
Hwrpt3bprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt3cPrm_py*pvrprm_py + Hwrpt3cprm_py*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt3cprm_pyPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt3aprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt3bprm_pyPrm_py*expMUexpnu

Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_py = deltaR*svprm_pyPrm_py
Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_py = snprm_pyPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt2fPrm_py*pvrprm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_py*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pyPrm_py + Hwrpt2gPrm_py*pnsqprm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_py*pnsqPrm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_py*pnsq

Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_py = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pyPrm_py + Hwrpt2cprm_pyPrm_py - Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_py)
Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_py*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_py = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pyPrm_py = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_py - Hwrpt3prm_pyPrm_py + Hwrpt4prm_pyPrm_py) + Hwrpt1Prm_py*(Hwrpt2prm_py - Hwrpt3prm_py + Hwrpt4prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_py*(Hwrpt2Prm_py - Hwrpt3Prm_py + Hwrpt4Prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_py*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_py
Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_py = pvr*svprm_pyPrm_py + pvrPrm_py*svprm_py + pvrprm_py*svPrm_py
Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_py = B*Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_py - Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_py = Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_py = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py*xi2 + pvrsqprm_pyPrm_py
Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_py = Hwcospt6Prm_py*pnprm_py + Hwcospt6prm_py*pnPrm_py + Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_py*pn
Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_py = Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_py*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pyPrm_py
Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_py = -B*Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_py + Hwcospt3*snprm_pyPrm_py + Hwcospt3Prm_py*snprm_py + Hwcospt3prm_py*snPrm_py + Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_py*sn
Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_py = Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_pyPrm_py = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + Hwcospt1Prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_py + Hwcospt1prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_py + Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_py*deltaTsqrtQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_py = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pyPrm_py + HSOLpt3Prm_py*s3prm_py + HSOLpt3prm_py*s3Prm_py
HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_py = HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_py*invxi2
HSOLprm_pyPrm_py = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + HSOLpt1Prm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_py + HSOLpt1prm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_py + HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py = deltaT*(Qprm_pyPrm_py + sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_py*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_py = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_py*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_py*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1prm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt1aPrm_py*sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt1aprm_py*sqrtQPrm_py
HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt2dPrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt2dprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py
HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_py = B*sxiprm_pyPrm_py
HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt1Prm_py*HSONLpt2bprm_py + HSONLpt1prm_py*HSONLpt2bPrm_py + HSONLpt1prm_pyPrm_py*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt2aPrm_py*svprm_py + HSONLpt2aprm_py*svPrm_py + HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_py*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pyPrm_py = pxir*svprm_pyPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*svprm_py + pxirprm_py*svPrm_py
HSONLpt3bprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt3cPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_py*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_pyPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt3bprm_pyPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pyPrm_py = B*HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_py - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_py
HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_py = snprm_pyPrm_py*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt4ePrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt4eprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt4dPrm_py*pxirprm_py + HSONLpt4dprm_py*pxirPrm_py + HSONLpt4dprm_pyPrm_py*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt4cprm_pyPrm_py*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pyPrm_py = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLpt3prm_pyPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pyPrm_py = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pyPrm_py + HSONLmultPrm_py*HSONLpt4prm_py + HSONLmultprm_py*HSONLpt4Prm_py + HSONLmultprm_pyPrm_py*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pyPrm_py = HSOLprm_pyPrm_py + HSONLprm_pyPrm_py + Hwcosprm_pyPrm_py*wcos + Hwrprm_pyPrm_py*wr + s3prm_pyPrm_py*w
Hsspt1prm_pyPrm_py = 3*sn*snprm_pyPrm_py + 3*snPrm_py*snprm_py - sx*sxprm_pyPrm_py - sxPrm_py*sxprm_py - sy*syprm_pyPrm_py - syPrm_py*syprm_py - sz*szprm_pyPrm_py - szPrm_py*szprm_py
Hssprm_pyPrm_py = Hsspt1prm_pyPrm_py*u3
Hprm_pyPrm_py = Hnsprm_pyPrm_py + Hsprm_pyPrm_py + Hssprm_pyPrm_py
Hrealprm_pyPrm_py = -HPrm_py*Hprm_py*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_py*Hprm_py*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pyPrm_py*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
pvrsqprm_pzPrm_py = 2*pvrPrm_py*pvrprm_pz
pnsqprm_pzPrm_py = 2*pnPrm_py*pnprm_pz
prsqprm_pzPrm_py = 2*prPrm_py*prprm_pz
pxirsqprm_pzPrm_py = 2*pxirPrm_py*pxirprm_pz
ptheta2prm_pzPrm_py = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pzPrm_py
prT4prm_pzPrm_py = 12*prT**2*prTPrm_py*prTprm_pz
Hnspt4prm_pzPrm_py = Hnspt5*prT4prm_pzPrm_py + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_py*pfprm_pz + Hnspt7*prsqprm_pzPrm_py + invrho2*ptheta2prm_pzPrm_py
Hnspt3prm_pzPrm_py = Hnspt4prm_pzPrm_py*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_pzPrm_py = Hnspt3prm_pzPrm_py*rho2
Hnsprm_pzPrm_py = Hnspt2prm_pzPrm_py*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2) - Hnspt2Prm_py*Hnspt2prm_pz*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(4*Hnspt2**2)
Qprm_pzPrm_py = Qpt1*pvrsqprm_pzPrm_py + Qpt2*pxirsqprm_pzPrm_py + Qpt3*pnsqprm_pzPrm_py
pn2prm_pzPrm_py = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_pzPrm_py
ppprm_pzPrm_py = Qprm_pzPrm_py
sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_py = r*(-36*pn2prm_pzPrm_py + 3*ppprm_pzPrm_py)
sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_py = r*(-30*pn2prm_pzPrm_py + 4*ppprm_pzPrm_py)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pzPrm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_py + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_py)

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pzPrm_py = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_pzPrm_py + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_pzPrm_py)

pp2prm_pzPrm_py = 2*pp*ppprm_pzPrm_py + 2*ppPrm_py*ppprm_pz
pn2u2prm_pzPrm_py = pn2prm_pzPrm_py*u2
ppu2prm_pzPrm_py = ppprm_pzPrm_py*u2
pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_py = pn2ppprm_pzPrm_py*u2
sMultiplier1pt6prm_pzPrm_py = -720*pn2*pn2prm_pzPrm_py - 720*pn2Prm_py*pn2prm_pz + 126*pn2ppprm_pzPrm_py + 3*pp2prm_pzPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt5prm_pzPrm_py = -96*pn2ppprm_pzPrm_py + 23*pp2prm_pzPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt4prm_pzPrm_py = 324*pn2prm_pzPrm_py - 120*ppprm_pzPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_pzPrm_py

sMultiplier1pt2prm_pzPrm_py = r*sMultiplier1pt4prm_pzPrm_py
sMultiplier1pt1prm_pzPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_pzPrm_py + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_pzPrm_py
sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_py = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1prm_pzPrm_py*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6prm_pzPrm_py = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_pzPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2Prm_py*pn2u2prm_pz/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_pz*pn2u2Prm_py/8 + 45*pn2prm_pzPrm_py*pn2u2/8
sMultiplier2pt5prm_pzPrm_py = pn2ppu2prm_pzPrm_py/4 - 5*pp2prm_pzPrm_py*u2/16

sMultiplier2pt2prm_pzPrm_py = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pzPrm_py
sMultiplier2pt1prm_pzPrm_py = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_pzPrm_py + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_pzPrm_py

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pzPrm_py + sMultiplier1prm_pzPrm_py*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pzPrm_py*sigmaKerr0

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pzPrm_py
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pzPrm_py
sxprm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pzPrm_py
syprm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pzPrm_py
szprm_pzPrm_py = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pzPrm_py
sxiprm_pzPrm_py = sxprm_pzPrm_py*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pzPrm_py*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pzPrm_py*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pzPrm_py = sxprm_pzPrm_py*vx + syprm_pzPrm_py*vy + szprm_pzPrm_py*vz
snprm_pzPrm_py = nx*sxprm_pzPrm_py + ny*syprm_pzPrm_py + nz*szprm_pzPrm_py

sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py = Qprm_pzPrm_py/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_py*Qprm_pz/(4*Q**(3/2))

oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py - sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_py = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py*sqrtQprm_pz + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pz*sqrtQPrm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py*sqrtQ

expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_py = expMUsq*(Qprm_pzPrm_py + sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py)
Hwrpt4aprm_pzPrm_py = pxirsq*svprm_pzPrm_py + pxirsqPrm_py*svprm_pz + pxirsqprm_pz*svPrm_py + pxirsqprm_pzPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt4prm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt4aprm_pzPrm_py*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cprm_pzPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pzPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*sxiPrm_py

Hwrpt3aprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt3bprm_pzPrm_py*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_pzPrm_py = B*Hwrpt3aprm_pzPrm_py
Hwrpt2gprm_pzPrm_py = deltaR*svprm_pzPrm_py
Hwrpt2fprm_pzPrm_py = snprm_pzPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt2fPrm_py*pvrprm_pz + Hwrpt2fprm_pz*pvrPrm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_pzPrm_py*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pzPrm_py + Hwrpt2gPrm_py*pnsqprm_pz + Hwrpt2gprm_pz*pnsqPrm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_pzPrm_py*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt2ePrm_py*pnprm_pz + Hwrpt2eprm_pz*pnPrm_py + Hwrpt2eprm_pzPrm_py*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_pzPrm_py = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_pzPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_py*svprm_pz + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pz*svPrm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pzPrm_py*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_pzPrm_py = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pzPrm_py + Hwrpt2cprm_pzPrm_py - Hwrpt2dprm_pzPrm_py)
Hwrpt2prm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt2aprm_pzPrm_py*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pzPrm_py = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pzPrm_py*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt1bprm_pzPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt1aprm_pzPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pzPrm_py = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pzPrm_py - Hwrpt3prm_pzPrm_py + Hwrpt4prm_pzPrm_py) + Hwrpt1Prm_py*(Hwrpt2prm_pz - Hwrpt3prm_pz + Hwrpt4prm_pz) + Hwrpt1prm_pz*(Hwrpt2Prm_py - Hwrpt3Prm_py + Hwrpt4Prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_pzPrm_py*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pzPrm_py = pxir*sxiprm_pzPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*sxiprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*sxiPrm_py
Hwcospt8prm_pzPrm_py = pvr*svprm_pzPrm_py + pvrPrm_py*svprm_pz + pvrprm_pz*svPrm_py
Hwcospt7prm_pzPrm_py = B*Hwcospt8prm_pzPrm_py - Hwcospt9prm_pzPrm_py*expMUexpnu

Hwcospt3prm_pzPrm_py = Hwcospt5prm_pzPrm_py*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pzPrm_py

Hwcospt1prm_pzPrm_py = Hwcospt2prm_pzPrm_py*invexpMUcubinvexpnu

deltaTsqrtQprm_pzPrm_py = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py

HSOLpt1prm_pzPrm_py = HSOLpt2prm_pzPrm_py*invxi2

HSONLpt2bprm_pzPrm_py = B*sxiprm_pzPrm_py
HSONLpt2aprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt2cprm_pzPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLpt1Prm_py*HSONLpt2bprm_pz + HSONLpt1prm_pz*HSONLpt2bPrm_py + HSONLpt1prm_pzPrm_py*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLpt2aPrm_py*svprm_pz + HSONLpt2aprm_pz*svPrm_py + HSONLpt2aprm_pzPrm_py*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pzPrm_py = pxir*svprm_pzPrm_py + pxirPrm_py*svprm_pz + pxirprm_pz*svPrm_py
HSONLpt3bprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLpt3cPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt3cprm_pz*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt3cprm_pzPrm_py*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt3bprm_pzPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pzPrm_py = B*HSONLpt2prm_pzPrm_py - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pzPrm_py
HSONLpt4eprm_pzPrm_py = snprm_pzPrm_py*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLpt4ePrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pz + HSONLpt4eprm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_py + HSONLpt4eprm_pzPrm_py*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt4dPrm_py*pxirprm_pz + HSONLpt4dprm_pz*pxirPrm_py + HSONLpt4dprm_pzPrm_py*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt4cprm_pzPrm_py*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLpt4bprm_pzPrm_py*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pzPrm_py = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLpt3prm_pzPrm_py*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pzPrm_py = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pzPrm_py + HSONLmultPrm_py*HSONLpt4prm_pz + HSONLmultprm_pz*HSONLpt4Prm_py + HSONLmultprm_pzPrm_py*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pzPrm_py = HSOLprm_pzPrm_py + HSONLprm_pzPrm_py + Hwcosprm_pzPrm_py*wcos + Hwrprm_pzPrm_py*wr + s3prm_pzPrm_py*w
Hsspt1prm_pzPrm_py = 3*sn*snprm_pzPrm_py + 3*snPrm_py*snprm_pz - sx*sxprm_pzPrm_py - sxPrm_py*sxprm_pz - sy*syprm_pzPrm_py - syPrm_py*syprm_pz - sz*szprm_pzPrm_py - szPrm_py*szprm_pz
Hssprm_pzPrm_py = Hsspt1prm_pzPrm_py*u3
Hprm_pzPrm_py = Hnsprm_pzPrm_py + Hsprm_pzPrm_py + Hssprm_pzPrm_py
Hrealprm_pzPrm_py = -HPrm_py*Hprm_pz*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_py*Hprm_pz*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pzPrm_py*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
prTPrm_pz = csi2*nz
prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz = prTPrm_pz*(1 - 1/csi1)
tmppxPrm_pz = -nx*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz
tmppyPrm_pz = -ny*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz
tmppzPrm_pz = -nz*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz + 1
pxirPrm_pz = r*(tmppxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz)
pvrPrm_pz = r*(tmppxPrm_pz*vx + tmppyPrm_pz*vy + tmppzPrm_pz*vz)
pvrsqPrm_pz = 2*pvr*pvrPrm_pz
pnPrm_pz = nx*tmppxPrm_pz + ny*tmppyPrm_pz + nz*tmppzPrm_pz
pnsqPrm_pz = 2*pn*pnPrm_pz
prPrm_pz = pnPrm_pz
prsqPrm_pz = 2*pr*prPrm_pz
pfPrm_pz = pxirPrm_pz
pxirsqPrm_pz = 2*pxir*pxirPrm_pz
ptheta2Prm_pz = invxi2*pvrsqPrm_pz
prT4Prm_pz = 4*prT**3*prTPrm_pz
Hnspt4Prm_pz = Hnspt5*prT4Prm_pz + 2*Hnspt6*pf*pfPrm_pz + Hnspt7*prsqPrm_pz + invrho2*ptheta2Prm_pz
Hnspt3Prm_pz = Hnspt4Prm_pz*deltaT
Hnspt2Prm_pz = Hnspt3Prm_pz*rho2
Hnspt1Prm_pz = pfPrm_pz*ww
HnsPrm_pz = Hnspt1Prm_pz*invLamb + Hnspt2Prm_pz*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2)
QPrm_pz = Qpt1*pvrsqPrm_pz + Qpt2*pxirsqPrm_pz + Qpt3*pnsqPrm_pz
pn2Prm_pz = deltaR*invrho2*prsqPrm_pz
ppPrm_pz = QPrm_pz
sKerrmultfactPrm_pz = r*(-36*pn2Prm_pz + 3*ppPrm_pz)
sStarmultfactPrm_pz = r*(-30*pn2Prm_pz + 4*ppPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1Prm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1Prm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1Prm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactPrm_pz)
pn2ppPrm_pz = pn2*ppPrm_pz + pn2Prm_pz*pp
pp2Prm_pz = 2*pp*ppPrm_pz
pn2u2Prm_pz = pn2Prm_pz*u2
ppu2Prm_pz = ppPrm_pz*u2
pn2ppu2Prm_pz = pn2ppPrm_pz*u2
sMultiplier1pt6Prm_pz = -720*pn2*pn2Prm_pz + 126*pn2ppPrm_pz + 3*pp2Prm_pz
sMultiplier1pt5Prm_pz = -96*pn2ppPrm_pz + 23*pp2Prm_pz
sMultiplier1pt4Prm_pz = 324*pn2Prm_pz - 120*ppPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt6Prm_pz
sMultiplier1pt3Prm_pz = -282*pn2Prm_pz + 206*ppPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt5Prm_pz
sMultiplier1pt2Prm_pz = r*sMultiplier1pt4Prm_pz
sMultiplier1pt1Prm_pz = eta*sMultiplier1pt2Prm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt3Prm_pz
sMultiplier1Prm_pz = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1Prm_pz*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6Prm_pz = 45*pn2*pn2u2Prm_pz/8 + 45*pn2Prm_pz*pn2u2/8 - 13*pn2ppu2Prm_pz/8
sMultiplier2pt5Prm_pz = pn2ppu2Prm_pz/4 - 5*pp2Prm_pz*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4Prm_pz = -49*pn2u2Prm_pz/8 + 17*ppu2Prm_pz/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6Prm_pz
sMultiplier2pt3Prm_pz = -2*pn2u2Prm_pz/3 - 109*ppu2Prm_pz/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5Prm_pz
sMultiplier2pt2Prm_pz = r*sMultiplier2pt4Prm_pz
sMultiplier2pt1Prm_pz = eta*sMultiplier2pt2Prm_pz + r*sMultiplier2pt3Prm_pz
sMultiplier2Prm_pz = eta*sMultiplier2pt1Prm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2Prm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1Prm_pz + sMultiplier1Prm_pz*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2Prm_pz*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2Prm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1Prm_pz + sMultiplier1Prm_pz*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2Prm_pz*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2Prm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1Prm_pz + sMultiplier1Prm_pz*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2Prm_pz*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2Prm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2Prm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2Prm_pz
sxPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExPrm_pz
syPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyPrm_pz
szPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzPrm_pz
sxiPrm_pz = sxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + syPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + szPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz
svPrm_pz = sxPrm_pz*vx + syPrm_pz*vy + szPrm_pz*vz
snPrm_pz = nx*sxPrm_pz + ny*syPrm_pz + nz*szPrm_pz
s3Prm_pz = e3USCOREx*sxPrm_pz + e3USCOREy*syPrm_pz + e3USCOREz*szPrm_pz
sqrtQPrm_pz = QPrm_pz/(2*sp.sqrt(Q))
oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz = 2*sqrtQPrm_pz
oneplus1sqrtQPrm_pz = oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz - sqrtQPrm_pz
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQPrm_pz + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_pz*sqrtQ
invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz = -twoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz/twoB1psqrtQsqrtQ**2
expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_pz = expMUsq*(QPrm_pz + sqrtQPrm_pz)
Hwrpt4aPrm_pz = pxirsq*svPrm_pz + pxirsqPrm_pz*sv
Hwrpt4Prm_pz = Hwrpt4aPrm_pz*expMUsqexpnusq
Hwrpt3cPrm_pz = pxir*sxiPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sxi
Hwrpt3bPrm_pz = Hwrpt3c*pvrPrm_pz + Hwrpt3cPrm_pz*pvr
Hwrpt3aPrm_pz = Hwrpt3bPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3Prm_pz = B*Hwrpt3aPrm_pz
Hwrpt2gPrm_pz = deltaR*svPrm_pz
Hwrpt2fPrm_pz = snPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2ePrm_pz = Hwrpt2f*pvrPrm_pz + Hwrpt2fPrm_pz*pvr
Hwrpt2dPrm_pz = Hwrpt2g*pnsqPrm_pz + Hwrpt2gPrm_pz*pnsq
Hwrpt2cPrm_pz = Hwrpt2e*pnPrm_pz + Hwrpt2ePrm_pz*pn
Hwrpt2bPrm_pz = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svPrm_pz + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*sv
Hwrpt2aPrm_pz = xi2*(Hwrpt2bPrm_pz + Hwrpt2cPrm_pz - Hwrpt2dPrm_pz)
Hwrpt2Prm_pz = Hwrpt2aPrm_pz*deltaT
Hwrpt1bPrm_pz = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz*invxi2
Hwrpt1aPrm_pz = Hwrpt1bPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1Prm_pz = Hwrpt1aPrm_pz*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
HwrPrm_pz = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2Prm_pz - Hwrpt3Prm_pz + Hwrpt4Prm_pz) + Hwrpt1Prm_pz*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9Prm_pz = pxir*sxiPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sxi
Hwcospt8Prm_pz = pvr*svPrm_pz + pvrPrm_pz*sv
Hwcospt7Prm_pz = B*Hwcospt8Prm_pz - Hwcospt9Prm_pz*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6Prm_pz = Hwcospt7Prm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5Prm_pz = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*xi2 + pvrsqPrm_pz
Hwcospt4Prm_pz = Hwcospt6*pnPrm_pz + Hwcospt6Prm_pz*pn
Hwcospt3Prm_pz = Hwcospt5Prm_pz*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqPrm_pz
Hwcospt2Prm_pz = -B*Hwcospt4Prm_pz + Hwcospt3*snPrm_pz + Hwcospt3Prm_pz*sn
Hwcospt1Prm_pz = Hwcospt2Prm_pz*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
HwcosPrm_pz = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz + Hwcospt1Prm_pz*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQPrm_pz = deltaT*sqrtQPrm_pz
invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQ**2
HSOLpt5Prm_pz = pxirPrm_pz*(-B + expMUexpnu)
HSOLpt4Prm_pz = HSOLpt5Prm_pz*invexpMU
HSOLpt3Prm_pz = HSOLpt4Prm_pz*expnusq
HSOLpt2Prm_pz = HSOLpt3*s3Prm_pz + HSOLpt3Prm_pz*s3
HSOLpt1Prm_pz = HSOLpt2Prm_pz*invxi2
HSOLPrm_pz = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_pz + HSOLpt1Prm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz = deltaT*(QPrm_pz + sqrtQPrm_pz)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2
HSONLmult2Prm_pz = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*invxi2
HSONLmultPrm_pz = HSONLmult2Prm_pz*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1bPrm_pz = pnPrm_pz*xi2
HSONLpt1aPrm_pz = HSONLpt1bPrm_pz*(-mucos + nucos) + mur*pvrPrm_pz - nur*pvrPrm_pz
HSONLpt1Prm_pz = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt1aPrm_pz*sqrtQ - HSONLpt1bPrm_pz*mucos + mur*pvrPrm_pz
HSONLpt2dPrm_pz = nur*pxirPrm_pz
HSONLpt2cPrm_pz = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt2dPrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt2bPrm_pz = B*sxiPrm_pz
HSONLpt2aPrm_pz = HSONLpt2cPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2Prm_pz = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bPrm_pz + HSONLpt1Prm_pz*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svPrm_pz + HSONLpt2aPrm_pz*sv
HSONLpt3cPrm_pz = pxir*svPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sv
HSONLpt3bPrm_pz = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt3cPrm_pz*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aPrm_pz = HSONLpt3bPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3Prm_pz = B*HSONLpt2Prm_pz - BR*HSONLpt3aPrm_pz
HSONLpt4ePrm_pz = snPrm_pz*xi2
HSONLpt4dPrm_pz = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt4ePrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cPrm_pz = HSONLpt4d*pxirPrm_pz + HSONLpt4dPrm_pz*pxir
HSONLpt4bPrm_pz = HSONLpt4cPrm_pz*nucos
HSONLpt4aPrm_pz = HSONLpt4bPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4Prm_pz = -B*HSONLpt4aPrm_pz + HSONLpt3Prm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLPrm_pz = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4Prm_pz + HSONLmultPrm_pz*HSONLpt4
HsPrm_pz = HSOLPrm_pz + HSONLPrm_pz + HwcosPrm_pz*wcos + HwrPrm_pz*wr + s3Prm_pz*w
Hsspt1Prm_pz = 3*sn*snPrm_pz - sx*sxPrm_pz - sy*syPrm_pz - sz*szPrm_pz
HssPrm_pz = Hsspt1Prm_pz*u3
HPrm_pz = HnsPrm_pz + HsPrm_pz + HssPrm_pz
HrealPrm_pz = HPrm_pz*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)

tmppxprm_xPrm_pz = -nx*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_pz - nxprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz
tmppyprm_xPrm_pz = -ny*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_pz - nyprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz
tmppzprm_xPrm_pz = -nz*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invprm_xPrm_pz - nzprm_x*prTtimesoneminuscsi1invPrm_pz
pxirprm_xPrm_pz = r*(tmppxPrm_pz*xiUSCORExprm_x + tmppxprm_xPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREyprm_x + tmppyprm_xPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_pz*xiUSCOREzprm_x + tmppzprm_xPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz) + rprm_x*(tmppxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + tmppyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + tmppzPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz)
pvrprm_xPrm_pz = r*(tmppxPrm_pz*vxprm_x + tmppxprm_xPrm_pz*vx + tmppyPrm_pz*vyprm_x + tmppyprm_xPrm_pz*vy + tmppzPrm_pz*vzprm_x + tmppzprm_xPrm_pz*vz) + rprm_x*(tmppxPrm_pz*vx + tmppyPrm_pz*vy + tmppzPrm_pz*vz)
pvrsqprm_xPrm_pz = 2*pvr*pvrprm_xPrm_pz + 2*pvrPrm_pz*pvrprm_x
pnprm_xPrm_pz = nx*tmppxprm_xPrm_pz + nxprm_x*tmppxPrm_pz + ny*tmppyprm_xPrm_pz + nyprm_x*tmppyPrm_pz + nz*tmppzprm_xPrm_pz + nzprm_x*tmppzPrm_pz
pnsqprm_xPrm_pz = 2*pn*pnprm_xPrm_pz + 2*pnPrm_pz*pnprm_x
prprm_xPrm_pz = pnprm_xPrm_pz
prsqprm_xPrm_pz = 2*pr*prprm_xPrm_pz + 2*prPrm_pz*prprm_x
pfprm_xPrm_pz = pxirprm_xPrm_pz
pxirsqprm_xPrm_pz = 2*pxir*pxirprm_xPrm_pz + 2*pxirPrm_pz*pxirprm_x
ptheta2prm_xPrm_pz = invxi2*pvrsqprm_xPrm_pz + invxi2prm_x*pvrsqPrm_pz
prT4prm_xPrm_pz = 4*prT**3*prTprm_xPrm_pz + 12*prT**2*prTPrm_pz*prTprm_x
Hnspt4prm_xPrm_pz = Hnspt5*prT4prm_xPrm_pz + Hnspt5prm_x*prT4Prm_pz + 2*Hnspt6*pf*pfprm_xPrm_pz + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_pz*pfprm_x + 2*Hnspt6prm_x*pf*pfPrm_pz + Hnspt7*prsqprm_xPrm_pz + Hnspt7prm_x*prsqPrm_pz + invrho2*ptheta2prm_xPrm_pz + invrho2prm_x*ptheta2Prm_pz
Hnspt3prm_xPrm_pz = Hnspt4Prm_pz*deltaTprm_x + Hnspt4prm_xPrm_pz*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_xPrm_pz = Hnspt3Prm_pz*rho2prm_x + Hnspt3prm_xPrm_pz*rho2
Hnspt1prm_xPrm_pz = pfPrm_pz*wwprm_x + pfprm_xPrm_pz*ww
Hnsprm_xPrm_pz = Hnspt1Prm_pz*invLambprm_x + Hnspt1prm_xPrm_pz*invLamb + sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)*(Hnspt2Prm_pz*invLambprm_x/2 + Hnspt2prm_xPrm_pz*invLamb/2)/(Hnspt2*invLamb) - Hnspt2Prm_pz*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)*(Hnspt2*invLambprm_x/2 + Hnspt2prm_x*invLamb/2)/(2*Hnspt2**2*invLamb)

pn2prm_xPrm_pz = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_xPrm_pz + deltaR*invrho2prm_x*prsqPrm_pz + deltaRprm_x*invrho2*prsqPrm_pz
ppprm_xPrm_pz = Qprm_xPrm_pz
sKerrmultfactprm_xPrm_pz = r*(-36*pn2prm_xPrm_pz + 3*ppprm_xPrm_pz) + rprm_x*(-36*pn2Prm_pz + 3*ppPrm_pz)
sStarmultfactprm_xPrm_pz = r*(-30*pn2prm_xPrm_pz + 4*ppprm_xPrm_pz) + rprm_x*(-30*pn2Prm_pz + 4*ppPrm_pz)

HSOLpt5prm_zPrm_pz = pxirPrm_pz*(-Bprm_z + expMUexpnuprm_z) + pxirprm_zPrm_pz*(-B + expMUexpnu)

Hrealprm_zPrm_pz = -HPrm_pz*Hprm_z*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_pz*Hprm_z*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_zPrm_pz*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)

pnsqprm_pxPrm_pz = 2*pnPrm_pz*pnprm_px

ptheta2prm_pxPrm_pz = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pxPrm_pz

Hnspt2prm_pxPrm_pz = Hnspt3prm_pxPrm_pz*rho2

ppprm_pxPrm_pz = Qprm_pxPrm_pz
sKerrmultfactprm_pxPrm_pz = r*(-36*pn2prm_pxPrm_pz + 3*ppprm_pxPrm_pz)

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pxPrm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_pxPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_pxPrm_pz)

deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pxPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pxPrm_pz + sMultiplier1prm_pxPrm_pz*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pxPrm_pz*sigmaKerr0

szprm_pxPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pxPrm_pz
sxiprm_pxPrm_pz = sxprm_pxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pxPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pxPrm_pz = sxprm_pxPrm_pz*vx + syprm_pxPrm_pz*vy + szprm_pxPrm_pz*vz

Hwrpt3cprm_pxPrm_pz = pxir*sxiprm_pxPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sxiprm_px + pxirprm_px*sxiPrm_pz
