deltaTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_pz*deltaTsqrtQprm_px/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pxPrm_pz = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pxPrm_pz + HSOLpt3Prm_pz*s3prm_px + HSOLpt3prm_px*s3Prm_pz
HSOLpt1prm_pxPrm_pz = HSOLpt2prm_pxPrm_pz*invxi2
HSOLprm_pxPrm_pz = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz + HSOLpt1Prm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_px + HSOLpt1prm_px*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_pz + HSOLpt1prm_pxPrm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_pz = deltaT*(Qprm_pxPrm_pz + sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_px/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_pz = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pxPrm_pz*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLmult2prm_pxPrm_pz*expnuinvexpMU2
HSONLpt1prm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt1a*sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt1aPrm_pz*sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt1aprm_px*sqrtQPrm_pz
HSONLpt2cprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt2dPrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt2dprm_px*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz
HSONLpt2bprm_pxPrm_pz = B*sxiprm_pxPrm_pz
HSONLpt2aprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt2cprm_pxPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt1Prm_pz*HSONLpt2bprm_px + HSONLpt1prm_px*HSONLpt2bPrm_pz + HSONLpt1prm_pxPrm_pz*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt2aPrm_pz*svprm_px + HSONLpt2aprm_px*svPrm_pz + HSONLpt2aprm_pxPrm_pz*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_pz = pxir*svprm_pxPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*svprm_px + pxirprm_px*svPrm_pz
HSONLpt3bprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt3c*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt3cPrm_pz*oneplus1sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt3cprm_px*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt3cprm_pxPrm_pz*oneplus1sqrtQ
HSONLpt3aprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt3bprm_pxPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pxPrm_pz = B*HSONLpt2prm_pxPrm_pz - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pxPrm_pz
HSONLpt4eprm_pxPrm_pz = snprm_pxPrm_pz*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt4ePrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQprm_px + HSONLpt4eprm_px*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt4eprm_pxPrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQ
HSONLpt4cprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt4dPrm_pz*pxirprm_px + HSONLpt4dprm_px*pxirPrm_pz + HSONLpt4dprm_pxPrm_pz*pxir
HSONLpt4bprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt4cprm_pxPrm_pz*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLpt4bprm_pxPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt4prm_pxPrm_pz = -B*HSONLpt4aprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLpt3prm_pxPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
HSONLprm_pxPrm_pz = HSONLmult*HSONLpt4prm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLmultPrm_pz*HSONLpt4prm_px + HSONLmultprm_px*HSONLpt4Prm_pz + HSONLmultprm_pxPrm_pz*HSONLpt4
Hsprm_pxPrm_pz = HSOLprm_pxPrm_pz + HSONLprm_pxPrm_pz + Hwcosprm_pxPrm_pz*wcos + Hwrprm_pxPrm_pz*wr + s3prm_pxPrm_pz*w
Hsspt1prm_pxPrm_pz = 3*sn*snprm_pxPrm_pz + 3*snPrm_pz*snprm_px - sx*sxprm_pxPrm_pz - sxPrm_pz*sxprm_px - sy*syprm_pxPrm_pz - syPrm_pz*syprm_px - sz*szprm_pxPrm_pz - szPrm_pz*szprm_px
Hssprm_pxPrm_pz = Hsspt1prm_pxPrm_pz*u3
Hprm_pxPrm_pz = Hnsprm_pxPrm_pz + Hsprm_pxPrm_pz + Hssprm_pxPrm_pz
Hrealprm_pxPrm_pz = -HPrm_pz*Hprm_px*eta**2*sp.sign(H)**2/(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)**(3/2) + 2*HPrm_pz*Hprm_px*eta*DiracDelta(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1) + Hprm_pxPrm_pz*eta*sp.sign(H)/sp.sqrt(2*eta*(sp.Abs(H) - 1) + 1)
pvrsqprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*pvrPrm_pz*pvrprm_py
pnsqprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*pnPrm_pz*pnprm_py
prsqprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*prPrm_pz*prprm_py
pxirsqprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*pxirPrm_pz*pxirprm_py
ptheta2prm_pyPrm_pz = invxi2*pvrsqprm_pyPrm_pz
prT4prm_pyPrm_pz = 12*prT**2*prTPrm_pz*prTprm_py
Hnspt4prm_pyPrm_pz = Hnspt5*prT4prm_pyPrm_pz + 2*Hnspt6*pfPrm_pz*pfprm_py + Hnspt7*prsqprm_pyPrm_pz + invrho2*ptheta2prm_pyPrm_pz
Hnspt3prm_pyPrm_pz = Hnspt4prm_pyPrm_pz*deltaT
Hnspt2prm_pyPrm_pz = Hnspt3prm_pyPrm_pz*rho2
Hnsprm_pyPrm_pz = Hnspt2prm_pyPrm_pz*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(2*Hnspt2) - Hnspt2Prm_pz*Hnspt2prm_py*sp.sqrt(Hnspt2*invLamb)/(4*Hnspt2**2)
Qprm_pyPrm_pz = Qpt1*pvrsqprm_pyPrm_pz + Qpt2*pxirsqprm_pyPrm_pz + Qpt3*pnsqprm_pyPrm_pz
pn2prm_pyPrm_pz = deltaR*invrho2*prsqprm_pyPrm_pz
ppprm_pyPrm_pz = Qprm_pyPrm_pz
sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz = r*(-36*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz + 3*ppprm_pyPrm_pz)
sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz = r*(-30*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz + 4*ppprm_pyPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pyPrm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREx*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREx*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pyPrm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREy*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREy*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz)
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pyPrm_pz = etaover12r*(sKerrUSCOREz*sKerrmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz + sStarUSCOREz*sStarmultfactprm_pyPrm_pz)
pn2ppprm_pyPrm_pz = pn2*ppprm_pyPrm_pz + pn2Prm_pz*ppprm_py + pn2prm_py*ppPrm_pz + pn2prm_pyPrm_pz*pp
pp2prm_pyPrm_pz = 2*pp*ppprm_pyPrm_pz + 2*ppPrm_pz*ppprm_py
pn2u2prm_pyPrm_pz = pn2prm_pyPrm_pz*u2
ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz = ppprm_pyPrm_pz*u2
pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz = pn2ppprm_pyPrm_pz*u2
sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_pz = -720*pn2*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz - 720*pn2Prm_pz*pn2prm_py + 126*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_pz + 3*pp2prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1pt5prm_pyPrm_pz = -96*pn2ppprm_pyPrm_pz + 23*pp2prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1pt4prm_pyPrm_pz = 324*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz - 120*ppprm_pyPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt6prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1pt3prm_pyPrm_pz = -282*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz + 206*ppprm_pyPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt5prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1pt2prm_pyPrm_pz = r*sMultiplier1pt4prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1pt1prm_pyPrm_pz = eta*sMultiplier1pt2prm_pyPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier1pt3prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_pz = -eta*sMultiplier1pt1prm_pyPrm_pz*u2/72
sMultiplier2pt6prm_pyPrm_pz = 45*pn2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_pz/8 + 45*pn2Prm_pz*pn2u2prm_py/8 - 13*pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz/8 + 45*pn2prm_py*pn2u2Prm_pz/8 + 45*pn2prm_pyPrm_pz*pn2u2/8
sMultiplier2pt5prm_pyPrm_pz = pn2ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz/4 - 5*pp2prm_pyPrm_pz*u2/16
sMultiplier2pt4prm_pyPrm_pz = -49*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_pz/8 + 17*ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz/12 + r*sMultiplier2pt6prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier2pt3prm_pyPrm_pz = -2*pn2u2prm_pyPrm_pz/3 - 109*ppu2prm_pyPrm_pz/36 + r*sMultiplier2pt5prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier2pt2prm_pyPrm_pz = r*sMultiplier2pt4prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier2pt1prm_pyPrm_pz = eta*sMultiplier2pt2prm_pyPrm_pz + r*sMultiplier2pt3prm_pyPrm_pz
sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_pz = eta*sMultiplier2pt1prm_pyPrm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx1prm_pyPrm_pz + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaStar0 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaKerr0
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy1prm_pyPrm_pz + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaStar1 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaKerr1
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz1prm_pyPrm_pz + sMultiplier1prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaStar2 + sMultiplier2prm_pyPrm_pz*sigmaKerr2
deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREx2prm_pyPrm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREy2prm_pyPrm_pz
deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREz2prm_pyPrm_pz
sxprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCORExprm_pyPrm_pz
syprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREyprm_pyPrm_pz
szprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaSigmaStarUSCOREzprm_pyPrm_pz
sxiprm_pyPrm_pz = sxprm_pyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREx + syprm_pyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREy + szprm_pyPrm_pz*xiUSCOREz
svprm_pyPrm_pz = sxprm_pyPrm_pz*vx + syprm_pyPrm_pz*vy + szprm_pyPrm_pz*vz
snprm_pyPrm_pz = nx*sxprm_pyPrm_pz + ny*syprm_pyPrm_pz + nz*szprm_pyPrm_pz
s3prm_pyPrm_pz = e3USCOREx*sxprm_pyPrm_pz + e3USCOREy*syprm_pyPrm_pz + e3USCOREz*szprm_pyPrm_pz
sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = Qprm_pyPrm_pz/(2*sp.sqrt(Q)) - QPrm_pz*Qprm_py/(4*Q**(3/2))
oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz
oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz - sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz
twoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQ*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQPrm_pz*sqrtQprm_py + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_py*sqrtQPrm_pz + 2*B*oneplus1sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz*sqrtQ

Hwrpt3cprm_pyPrm_pz = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_pz

Hwrpt3aprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt3bprm_pyPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
Hwrpt3prm_pyPrm_pz = B*Hwrpt3aprm_pyPrm_pz
Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaR*svprm_pyPrm_pz
Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_pz = snprm_pyPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt2eprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt2fPrm_pz*pvrprm_py + Hwrpt2fprm_py*pvrPrm_pz + Hwrpt2fprm_pyPrm_pz*pvr
Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt2g*pnsqprm_pyPrm_pz + Hwrpt2gPrm_pz*pnsqprm_py + Hwrpt2gprm_py*pnsqPrm_pz + Hwrpt2gprm_pyPrm_pz*pnsq
Hwrpt2cprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt2ePrm_pz*pnprm_py + Hwrpt2eprm_py*pnPrm_pz + Hwrpt2eprm_pyPrm_pz*pn
Hwrpt2bprm_pyPrm_pz = expMUsqsqrtQplusQ*svprm_pyPrm_pz + expMUsqsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*svprm_py + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_py*svPrm_pz + expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz*sv
Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_pz = xi2*(Hwrpt2bprm_pyPrm_pz + Hwrpt2cprm_pyPrm_pz - Hwrpt2dprm_pyPrm_pz)
Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt2aprm_pyPrm_pz*deltaT
Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_pz = invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz*invxi2
Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt1bprm_pyPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt1aprm_pyPrm_pz*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwrprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwrpt1*(Hwrpt2prm_pyPrm_pz - Hwrpt3prm_pyPrm_pz + Hwrpt4prm_pyPrm_pz) + Hwrpt1Prm_pz*(Hwrpt2prm_py - Hwrpt3prm_py + Hwrpt4prm_py) + Hwrpt1prm_py*(Hwrpt2Prm_pz - Hwrpt3Prm_pz + Hwrpt4Prm_pz) + Hwrpt1prm_pyPrm_pz*(Hwrpt2 - Hwrpt3 + Hwrpt4)
Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_pz = pxir*sxiprm_pyPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*sxiprm_py + pxirprm_py*sxiPrm_pz
Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_pz = pvr*svprm_pyPrm_pz + pvrPrm_pz*svprm_py + pvrprm_py*svPrm_pz
Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_pz = B*Hwcospt8prm_pyPrm_pz - Hwcospt9prm_pyPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwcospt7prm_pyPrm_pz*sqrtdeltaR
Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_pz = -expMUsqsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz*xi2 + pvrsqprm_pyPrm_pz
Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwcospt6Prm_pz*pnprm_py + Hwcospt6prm_py*pnPrm_pz + Hwcospt6prm_pyPrm_pz*pn
Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwcospt5prm_pyPrm_pz*deltaT - expMUsqexpnusq*pxirsqprm_pyPrm_pz
Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_pz = -B*Hwcospt4prm_pyPrm_pz + Hwcospt3*snprm_pyPrm_pz + Hwcospt3Prm_pz*snprm_py + Hwcospt3prm_py*snPrm_pz + Hwcospt3prm_pyPrm_pz*sn
Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_pz = Hwcospt2prm_pyPrm_pz*invexpMUcubinvexpnu
Hwcosprm_pyPrm_pz = Hwcospt1*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz + Hwcospt1Prm_pz*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQprm_py + Hwcospt1prm_py*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQPrm_pz + Hwcospt1prm_pyPrm_pz*invtwoB1psqrtQsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaT*sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz
invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQPrm_pz*deltaTsqrtQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQ**3
HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_pz = HSOLpt3*s3prm_pyPrm_pz + HSOLpt3Prm_pz*s3prm_py + HSOLpt3prm_py*s3Prm_pz
HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_pz = HSOLpt2prm_pyPrm_pz*invxi2
HSOLprm_pyPrm_pz = HSOLpt1*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz + HSOLpt1Prm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQprm_py + HSOLpt1prm_py*invdeltatTsqrtQPrm_pz + HSOLpt1prm_pyPrm_pz*invdeltatTsqrtQ
deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz = deltaT*(Qprm_pyPrm_pz + sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz)
invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz = -deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**2 + 2*deltaTsqrtQplusQPrm_pz*deltaTsqrtQplusQprm_py/deltaTsqrtQplusQ**3
HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_pz = invdeltaTsqrtQplusQprm_pyPrm_pz*invxi2
HSONLmultprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLmult2prm_pyPrm_pz*expnuinvexpMU2

HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt2d*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz + HSONLpt2dPrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt2dprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz
HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_pz = B*sxiprm_pyPrm_pz
HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt2cprm_pyPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt1*HSONLpt2bprm_pyPrm_pz + HSONLpt1Prm_pz*HSONLpt2bprm_py + HSONLpt1prm_py*HSONLpt2bPrm_pz + HSONLpt1prm_pyPrm_pz*HSONLpt2b + HSONLpt2a*svprm_pyPrm_pz + HSONLpt2aPrm_pz*svprm_py + HSONLpt2aprm_py*svPrm_pz + HSONLpt2aprm_pyPrm_pz*sv
HSONLpt3cprm_pyPrm_pz = pxir*svprm_pyPrm_pz + pxirPrm_pz*svprm_py + pxirprm_py*svPrm_pz

HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt3bprm_pyPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
HSONLpt3prm_pyPrm_pz = B*HSONLpt2prm_pyPrm_pz - BR*HSONLpt3aprm_pyPrm_pz
HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_pz = snprm_pyPrm_pz*xi2
HSONLpt4dprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt4e*oneplus2sqrtQprm_pyPrm_pz + HSONLpt4ePrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQprm_py + HSONLpt4eprm_py*oneplus2sqrtQPrm_pz + HSONLpt4eprm_pyPrm_pz*oneplus2sqrtQ

HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt4cprm_pyPrm_pz*nucos
HSONLpt4aprm_pyPrm_pz = HSONLpt4bprm_pyPrm_pz*expMUexpnu
